00001| #![cfg_attr(target_arch = "wasm32", no_main)]
00002| 
00003| mod state;
00004| 
00005| use linera_sdk::{
00006|     abi::WithContractAbi,
00007|     views::{RootView, View},
00008|     Contract, ContractRuntime,
00009| };
00010| 
00011| use linera_name_system::Operation;
00012| use self::state::LineraNameSystemState;
00013| 
00014| pub struct LineraNameSystemContract {
00015|     state: LineraNameSystemState,
00016|     runtime: ContractRuntime<Self>,
00017| }
00018| 
00019| linera_sdk::contract!(LineraNameSystemContract);
00020| 
00021| impl WithContractAbi for LineraNameSystemContract {
00022|     type Abi = linera_name_system::LineraNameSystemAbi;
00023| }
00024| 
00025| impl Contract for LineraNameSystemContract {
00026|     type Message = ();
00027|     type Parameters = ();
00028|     type InstantiationArgument = ();
00029|     type EventValue = ();
00030| 
00031|     async fn load(runtime: ContractRuntime<Self>) -> Self {
00032|         let state = LineraNameSystemState::load(runtime.root_view_storage_context())
00033|             .await
00034|             .expect("Failed to load state");
00035|         LineraNameSystemContract { state, runtime }
00036|     }
00037| 
00038|     async fn instantiate(&mut self, _argument: Self::InstantiationArgument) {
00039|         // No initialization needed
00040|     }
00041| 
00042|     async fn execute_operation(&mut self, operation: Self::Operation) -> Self::Response {
00043|         let owner = self.runtime.authenticated_signer()
00044|             .expect("Operation must be signed")
00045|             .to_string();
00046| 
00047|         match operation {
00048|             Operation::Register { name } => {
00049|                 // Validate domain name
00050|                 assert!(!name.is_empty(), "Domain name cannot be empty");
00051|                 assert!(name.len() <= 63, "Domain name too long");
00052|                 assert!(
00053|                     name.chars().all(|c| c.is_ascii_alphanumeric() || c == '-'),
00054|                     "Invalid characters in domain name"
00055|                 );
00056| 
00057|                 // Check if domain is available
00058|                 let existing = self.state.domains.get(&name).await.expect("Failed to read state");
00059|                 assert!(existing.is_none(), "Domain already registered");
00060| 
00061|                 // Register the domain
00062|                 self.state.domains.insert(&name, owner).expect("Failed to register domain");
00063|             }
00064|             Operation::Transfer { name, new_owner } => {
00065|                 // Check ownership
00066|                 let current_owner = self.state.domains.get(&name).await
00067|                     .expect("Failed to read state")
00068|                     .expect("Domain not registered");
00069|                 assert_eq!(current_owner, owner, "Not the domain owner");
00070| 
00071|                 // Transfer ownership
00072|                 self.state.domains.insert(&name, new_owner).expect("Failed to transfer domain");
00073|             }
00074|         }
00075|     }
00076| 
00077|     async fn execute_message(&mut self, _message: Self::Message) {
00078|         // No cross-chain messages
00079|     }
00080| 
00081|     async fn store(mut self) {
00082|         self.state.save().await.expect("Failed to save state");
00083|     }
00084| }

<file>
00001| #![cfg_attr(target_arch = "wasm32", no_main)]
00002| 
00003| mod state;
00004| 
00005| use async_graphql::{EmptySubscription, Object, Request, Response, Schema};
00006| use linera_sdk::{
00007|     abi::WithServiceAbi,
00008|     views::View,
00009|     Service, ServiceRuntime,
00010| };
00011| use std::sync::Arc;
00012| 
00013| use linera_name_system::Operation;
00014| use self::state::LineraNameSystemState;
00015| 
00016| pub struct LineraNameSystemService {
00017|     state: Arc<LineraNameSystemState>,
00018|     runtime: Arc<ServiceRuntime<Self>>,
00019| }
00020| 
00021| linera_sdk::service!(LineraNameSystemService);
00022| 
00023| impl WithServiceAbi for LineraNameSystemService {
00024|     type Abi = linera_name_system::LineraNameSystemAbi;
00025| }
00026| 
00027| impl Service for LineraNameSystemService {
00028|     type Parameters = ();
00029| 
00030|     async fn new(runtime: ServiceRuntime<Self>) -> Self {
00031|         let state = LineraNameSystemState::load(runtime.root_view_storage_context())
00032|             .await
00033|             .expect("Failed to load state");
00034|         LineraNameSystemService { 
00035|             state: Arc::new(state),
00036|             runtime: Arc::new(runtime),
00037|         }
00038|     }
00039| 
00040|     async fn handle_query(&self, request: Request) -> Response {
00041|         let schema = Schema::build(QueryRoot, MutationRoot, EmptySubscription)
00042|             .data(self.state.clone())
00043|             .data(self.runtime.clone())
00044|             .finish();
00045|         schema.execute(request).await
00046|     }
00047| }
00048| 
00049| struct QueryRoot;
00050| 
00051| #[Object]
00052| impl QueryRoot {
00053|     /// Look up the owner of a domain
00054|     async fn owner(&self, ctx: &async_graphql::Context<'_>, name: String) -> Option<String> {
00055|         let state = ctx.data_unchecked::<Arc<LineraNameSystemState>>();
00056|         state.domains.get(&name).await.ok().flatten()
00057|     }
00058| 
00059|     /// Check if a domain is available
00060|     async fn is_available(&self, ctx: &async_graphql::Context<'_>, name: String) -> bool {
00061|         let state = ctx.data_unchecked::<Arc<LineraNameSystemState>>();
00062|         state.domains.get(&name).await.ok().flatten().is_none()
00063|     }
00064| }
00065| 
00066| struct MutationRoot;
00067| 
00068| #[Object]
00069| impl MutationRoot {
00070|     /// Register a new .linera domain
00071|     async fn register(&self, ctx: &async_graphql::Context<'_>, name: String) -> bool {
00072|         let runtime = ctx.data_unchecked::<Arc<ServiceRuntime<LineraNameSystemService>>>();
00073|         let operation = Operation::Register { name };
00074|         runtime.schedule_operation(&operation);
00075|         true
00076|     }
00077| 
00078|     /// Transfer domain ownership
00079|     async fn transfer(&self, ctx: &async_graphql::Context<'_>, name: String, new_owner: String) -> bool {
00080|         let runtime = ctx.data_unchecked::<Arc<ServiceRuntime<LineraNameSystemService>>>();
00081|         let operation = Operation::Transfer { name, new_owner };
00082|         runtime.schedule_operation(&operation);
00083|         true
00084|     }
00085| }
00086|

<file>
00001| "use client";
00002| 
00003| import { useCallback, useEffect, useRef, useState } from "react";
00004| import { useDynamicContext, useIsLoggedIn } from "@dynamic-labs/sdk-react-core";
00005| import { DynamicWidget } from "@dynamic-labs/sdk-react-core";
00006| import { lineraAdapter, type LineraProvider } from "@/lib/linera-adapter";
00007| 
00008| interface BlockLog {
00009|     height: number;
00010|     hash: string;
00011| }
00012| 
00013| interface DomainQueryResult {
00014|     Owner?: string | null;
00015|     IsAvailable?: boolean;
00016| }
00017| 
00018| export default function CounterApp() {
00019|     const { primaryWallet } = useDynamicContext();
00020|     const isLoggedIn = useIsLoggedIn();
00021|     const [mounted, setMounted] = useState(false);
00022|     const [chainId, setChainId] = useState<string | null>(null);
00023|     const [logs, setLogs] = useState<BlockLog[]>([]);
00024|     const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
00025| 
00026|     const providerRef = useRef<LineraProvider | null>(null);
00027|     const [chainConnected, setChainConnected] = useState(false);
00028|     const [appConnected, setAppConnected] = useState(false);
00029|     const [isAutoConnecting, setIsAutoConnecting] = useState(false);
00030| 
00031|     // Domain registration state
00032|     const [domainName, setDomainName] = useState("");
00033|     const [searchResult, setSearchResult] = useState<DomainQueryResult | null>(null);
00034|     const [isSearching, setIsSearching] = useState(false);
00035|     const [isRegistering, setIsRegistering] = useState(false);
00036| 
00037|     const applicationId = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_LINERA_APPLICATION_ID || "";
00038| 
00039|     useEffect(() => {
00040|         setMounted(true);
00041|         setChainConnected(lineraAdapter.isChainConnected());
00042|         setAppConnected(lineraAdapter.isApplicationSet());
00043|     }, []);
00044| 
00045|     // Auto-connect to Linera when wallet is connected
00046|     const autoConnect = useCallback(async () => {
00047|         if (!primaryWallet || !applicationId || isAutoConnecting) return;
00048|         if (chainConnected && appConnected) return;
00049| 
00050|         setIsAutoConnecting(true);
00051|         setError(null);
00052| 
00053|         try {
00054|             // Connect to Linera chain
00055|             if (!chainConnected) {
00056|                 const provider = await lineraAdapter.connect(primaryWallet);
00057|                 providerRef.current = provider;
00058|                 setChainConnected(true);
00059|                 setChainId(provider.chainId);
00060|             }
00061| 
00062|             // Connect to application
00063|             if (!appConnected && applicationId) {
00064|                 await lineraAdapter.setApplication(applicationId);
00065|                 setAppConnected(true);
00066|             }
00067|         } catch (err) {
00068|             console.error("Auto-connect failed:", err);
00069|             setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Failed to auto-connect to Linera");
00070|         } finally {
00071|             setIsAutoConnecting(false);
00072|         }
00073|     }, [primaryWallet, applicationId, chainConnected, appConnected, isAutoConnecting]);
00074| 
00075|     useEffect(() => {
00076|         if (mounted && isLoggedIn && primaryWallet && !chainConnected) {
00077|             autoConnect();
00078|         }
00079|     }, [mounted, isLoggedIn, primaryWallet, chainConnected, autoConnect]);
00080| 
00081|     // Reset Linera adapter when Dynamic wallet disconnects
00082|     useEffect(() => {
00083|         if (!isLoggedIn || !primaryWallet) {
00084|             lineraAdapter.reset();
00085|             providerRef.current = null;
00086|             setChainConnected(false);
00087|             setAppConnected(false);
00088|             setChainId(null);
00089|             setLogs([]);
00090|             setError(null);
00091|             setSearchResult(null);
00092|         }
00093|     }, [isLoggedIn, primaryWallet]);
00094| 
00095|     useEffect(() => {
00096|         if (!chainConnected || !providerRef.current) return;
00097|         const client = providerRef.current.client;
00098|         if (!client || typeof client.onNotification !== 'function') return;
00099| 
00100|         const handler = (notification: unknown) => {
00101|             const newBlock: BlockLog | undefined = (
00102|                 notification as { reason: { NewBlock: BlockLog } }
00103|             )?.reason?.NewBlock;
00104|             if (!newBlock) return;
00105|             setLogs((prev) => [newBlock, ...prev]);
00106|         };
00107| 
00108|         try {
00109|             client.onNotification(handler);
00110|         } catch (err) {
00111|             console.error('Failed to set notification handler:', err);
00112|         }
00113|         return () => { };
00114|     }, [chainConnected]);
00115| 
00116|     async function handleCheckDomain() {
00117|         if (!domainName.trim()) {
00118|             setError("Please enter a domain name");
00119|             return;
00120|         }
00121|         setIsSearching(true);
00122|         setError(null);
00123|         setSearchResult(null);
00124| 
00125|         try {
00126|             // GraphQL query for availability
00127|             const result = await lineraAdapter.queryApplication<{
00128|                 data?: { isAvailable: boolean };
00129|                 errors?: Array<{ message: string }>;
00130|             }>({
00131|                 query: `query { isAvailable(name: "${domainName.trim()}") }`
00132|             });
00133|             if (result.errors?.length) {
00134|                 throw new Error(result.errors[0].message);
00135|             }
00136|             setSearchResult({ IsAvailable: result.data?.isAvailable });
00137|         } catch (err) {
00138|             console.error("Failed to check domain:", err);
00139|             setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Failed to check domain availability");
00140|         } finally {
00141|             setIsSearching(false);
00142|         }
00143|     }
00144| 
00145|     async function handleRegisterDomain() {
00146|         if (!domainName.trim()) {
00147|             setError("Please enter a domain name");
00148|             return;
00149|         }
00150|         setIsRegistering(true);
00151|         setError(null);
00152| 
00153|         try {
00154|             // Call the register mutation - the service will schedule the operation
00155|             const result = await lineraAdapter.queryApplication<{
00156|                 data?: { register: boolean };
00157|                 errors?: Array<{ message: string }>;
00158|             }>({
00159|                 query: `mutation { register(name: "${domainName.trim()}") }`
00160|             });
00161| 
00162|             if (result.errors?.length) {
00163|                 throw new Error(result.errors[0].message);
00164|             }
00165| 
00166|             if (result.data?.register) {
00167|                 // Registration operation scheduled successfully
00168|                 setSearchResult({ IsAvailable: false });
00169|                 setError(null);
00170|                 // Show success message
00171|                 alert(`Domain ${domainName.trim()}.linera registration submitted! It may take a moment to be confirmed.`);
00172|             }
00173|         } catch (err) {
00174|             console.error("Failed to register domain:", err);
00175|             setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Failed to register domain");
00176|         } finally {
00177|             setIsRegistering(false);
00178|         }
00179|     }
00180| 
00181|     async function handleLookupOwner() {
00182|         if (!domainName.trim()) {
00183|             setError("Please enter a domain name");
00184|             return;
00185|         }
00186|         setIsSearching(true);
00187|         setError(null);
00188|         setSearchResult(null);
00189| 
00190|         try {
00191|             // GraphQL query for owner
00192|             const result = await lineraAdapter.queryApplication<{
00193|                 data?: { owner: string | null };
00194|                 errors?: Array<{ message: string }>;
00195|             }>({
00196|                 query: `query { owner(name: "${domainName.trim()}") }`
00197|             });
00198|             if (result.errors?.length) {
00199|                 throw new Error(result.errors[0].message);
00200|             }
00201|             setSearchResult({ Owner: result.data?.owner });
00202|         } catch (err) {
00203|             console.error("Failed to lookup owner:", err);
00204|             setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Failed to lookup domain owner");
00205|         } finally {
00206|             setIsSearching(false);
00207|         }
00208|     }
00209| 
00210|     return (
00211|         <div className="flex min-h-screen items-center justify-center bg-zinc-50 font-sans dark:bg-black">
00212|             <div className="w-full max-w-3xl px-6 py-12">
00213|                 <div className="rounded-xl bg-white p-8 shadow-lg dark:bg-zinc-900">
00214|                     <div className="mb-8 flex items-center justify-between">
00215|                         <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold text-zinc-900 dark:text-white">Linera Name System</h1>
00216|                         <DynamicWidget />
00217|                     </div>
00218| 
00219|                     <div className="mb-8">
00220|                         <p className="mb-2 text-zinc-600 dark:text-zinc-400">
00221|                             Register your unique .linera domain on the Linera blockchain.
00222|                         </p>
00223|                         <p className="text-zinc-600 dark:text-zinc-400">
00224|                             Connect your wallet to get started. Your chain will be automatically claimed from the testnet faucet.
00225|                         </p>
00226|                     </div>
00227| 
00228|                     {error && (
00229|                         <div className="mb-6 rounded-lg bg-red-50 p-4 dark:bg-red-900/20">
00230|                             <p className="text-red-500 dark:text-red-300">{error}</p>
00231|                         </div>
00232|                     )}
00233| 
00234|                     {/* Connection Status */}
00235|                     {mounted && isAutoConnecting && (
00236|                         <div className="mb-6 flex items-center justify-center gap-2 rounded-lg bg-sky-50 p-4 dark:bg-sky-900/20">
00237|                             <div className="h-4 w-4 animate-spin rounded-full border-2 border-sky-600 border-t-transparent" />
00238|                             <p className="text-sky-600 dark:text-sky-400">Connecting to Linera testnet...</p>
00239|                         </div>
00240|                     )}
00241|

00246|                             </p>
00247|                         </div>

00249| 
00250|                     {/* Domain Registration UI */}
00251|                     {chainConnected && appConnected && (
00252|                         <div className="space-y-6">
00253|                             <div className="rounded-lg bg-zinc-100 p-6 dark:bg-zinc-800">
00254|                                 <h2 className="mb-4 text-lg font-semibold text-zinc-900 dark:text-white">

00256|                                 </h2>

00013|   "99f357923c7e3afe8bfa4355af2d835482f7920cf918eb08ef76a5dd7451177b";
00014|

00024|   private static instance: LineraAdapter | null = null;
00025|   private provider: LineraProvider | null = null;
00026|   private application: Application | null = null;
00027| 
00028|   private connectPromise: Promise<LineraProvider> | null = null;
00029|   private onConnectionChange?: () => void;
00030|

00032|

00034|     if (!LineraAdapter.instance) LineraAdapter.instance = new LineraAdapter();
00035|     return LineraAdapter.instance;

00038|   async connect(
00039|     dynamicWallet: DynamicWallet,
00040|     rpcUrl?: string
00041|   ): Promise<LineraProvider> {
00042|     if (this.provider) return this.provider;
00043|     if (this.connectPromise) return this.connectPromise;
00044| 
00045|     if (!dynamicWallet) {
00046|       throw new Error("Dynamic wallet is required for Linera connection");

00051|         const { address } = dynamicWallet;
00052|         console.log("ðŸ”— Connecting with Dynamic wallet:", address);
00053| 
00054|         // Load Linera from public folder to avoid file:// URL issues
00055|         const linera = await loadLinera();
00056|         console.log("âœ… Linera WASM modules initialized successfully");
00057| 
00058|         const faucet = new linera.Faucet(rpcUrl || LINERA_RPC_URL);
00059|         const wallet = await faucet.createWallet();
00060|         const chainId = await faucet.claimChain(wallet, address);
00061| 
00062|         const signer = new DynamicSigner(dynamicWallet);
00063|         // Third parameter is skip_process_inbox (false = process inbox)
00064|         // Client constructor may return a Promise in WASM bindings
00065|         const client = await Promise.resolve(new linera.Client(wallet, signer, true));
00066|         console.log("âœ… Linera wallet created successfully!");
00067|         console.log("ðŸ” Client methods:", Object.keys(client), typeof client.frontend);
00068|

00070|           client,
00071|           wallet,
00072|           faucet,
00073|           chainId,
00074|           address: dynamicWallet.address,
00075|         };
00076| 
00077|         this.onConnectionChange?.();
00078|         return this.provider;
00079|       })();
00080| 
00081|       const provider = await this.connectPromise;
00082|       return provider;
00083|     } catch (error) {
00084|       console.error("Failed to connect to Linera:", error);
00085|       throw new Error(
00086|         `Failed to connect to Linera network: ${error instanceof Error ? error.message : "Unknown error"
00087|         }`
00088|       );
00089|     } finally {
00090|       this.connectPromise = null;
00091|     }
00092|   }

## Assistant

Let me implement the cross-chain messaging pattern for the Linera Name System. The deploying chain will be the Registry Chain (source of truth).

**Tool Call: contracts/linera_name_system/src/lib.rs**
Status: Completed



Diff: [PROJECT_ROOT]/linera-name-system/contracts/linera_name_system/src/lib.rs
```
use async_graphql::{Request, Response};
use linera_sdk::abi::{ContractAbi, ServiceAbi};
use linera_sdk::base::ChainId;
use serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};

pub struct LineraNameSystemAbi;

impl ContractAbi for LineraNameSystemAbi {
    type Operation = Operation;
    type Response = ();
}

impl ServiceAbi for LineraNameSystemAbi {
    type Query = Request;
    type QueryResponse = Response;
}

/// Operations that can be executed by the contract.
#[derive(Debug, Deserialize, Serialize)]
pub enum Operation {
    /// Register a new .linera domain (sends message to registry chain)
    Register { name: String },
    /// Transfer domain ownership (sends message to registry chain)
    Transfer { name: String, new_owner: String },
}

/// Cross-chain messages for the name system.
#[derive(Debug, Deserialize, Serialize)]
pub enum Message {
    /// Request to register a domain on the registry chain
    RequestRegister {
        name: String,
        owner: String,
        requester_chain: ChainId,
    },
    /// Request to transfer a domain on the registry chain
    RequestTransfer {
        name: String,
        new_owner: String,
        current_owner: String,
        requester_chain: ChainId,
    },
    /// Response: Registration successful
    RegistrationSuccess { name: String },
    /// Response: Registration failed (domain taken)
    RegistrationFailed { name: String, reason: String },
    /// Response: Transfer successful
    TransferSuccess { name: String, new_owner: String },
    /// Response: Transfer failed
    TransferFailed { name: String, reason: String },
}
```

use linera_sdk::base::ChainId;
use linera_sdk::views::{MapView, RegisterView, RootView, ViewStorageContext};

/// The application state storing domain registrations.
#[derive(RootView)]
#[view(context = ViewStorageContext)]
pub struct LineraNameSystemState {
    /// Map of domain names to owner addresses (global registry on registry chain)
    pub domains: MapView<String, String>,
    /// The registry chain ID (set during instantiation on the deploying chain)
    pub registry_chain_id: RegisterView<Option<ChainId>>,
}
```


**Tool Call: contracts/linera_name_system/src/contract.rs**
Status: Completed



Diff: [PROJECT_ROOT]/linera-name-system/contracts/linera_name_system/src/contract.rs
```
#![cfg_attr(target_arch = "wasm32", no_main)]

mod state;

use linera_sdk::{
    abi::WithContractAbi,
    base::ChainId,
    views::{RootView, View},
    Contract, ContractRuntime,
};

use linera_name_system::{Message, Operation};
use self::state::LineraNameSystemState;

pub struct LineraNameSystemContract {
    state: LineraNameSystemState,
    runtime: ContractRuntime<Self>,
}

linera_sdk::contract!(LineraNameSystemContract);

impl WithContractAbi for LineraNameSystemContract {
    type Abi = linera_name_system::LineraNameSystemAbi;
}

impl Contract for LineraNameSystemContract {
    type Message = Message;
    type Parameters = ();
    type InstantiationArgument = ();
    type EventValue = ();

    async fn load(runtime: ContractRuntime<Self>) -> Self {
        let state = LineraNameSystemState::load(runtime.root_view_storage_context())
            .await
            .expect("Failed to load state");
        LineraNameSystemContract { state, runtime }
    }

    async fn instantiate(&mut self, _argument: Self::InstantiationArgument) {
        // Set the registry chain ID to the chain that deploys the application
        // This chain becomes the "source of truth" for all domain registrations
        let registry_chain_id = self.runtime.chain_id();
        self.state.registry_chain_id.set(Some(registry_chain_id));
    }

    async fn execute_operation(&mut self, operation: Self::Operation) -> Self::Response {
        let owner = self.runtime.authenticated_signer()
            .expect("Operation must be signed")
            .to_string();
        
        let current_chain = self.runtime.chain_id();
        let registry_chain_id = self.state.registry_chain_id.get()
            .expect("Registry chain ID not set");

        match operation {
            Operation::Register { name } => {
                // Validate domain name
                assert!(!name.is_empty(), "Domain name cannot be empty");
                assert!(name.len() <= 63, "Domain name too long");
                assert!(
                    name.chars().all(|c| c.is_ascii_alphanumeric() || c == '-'),
                    "Invalid characters in domain name"
                );

                if current_chain == registry_chain_id {
                    // We ARE the registry chain - register directly
                    let existing = self.state.domains.get(&name).await.expect("Failed to read state");
                    assert!(existing.is_none(), "Domain already registered");
                    self.state.domains.insert(&name, owner).expect("Failed to register domain");
                } else {
                    // Send registration request to registry chain
                    let message = Message::RequestRegister {
                        name,
                        owner,
                        requester_chain: current_chain,
                    };
                    self.runtime.send_message(registry_chain_id, message);
                }
            }
            Operation::Transfer { name, new_owner } => {
                if current_chain == registry_chain_id {
                    // We ARE the registry chain - transfer directly
                    let current_owner = self.state.domains.get(&name).await
                        .expect("Failed to read state")
                        .expect("Domain not registered");
                    assert_eq!(current_owner, owner, "Not the domain owner");
                    self.state.domains.insert(&name, new_owner).expect("Failed to transfer domain");
                } else {
                    // Send transfer request to registry chain
                    let message = Message::RequestTransfer {
                        name,
                        new_owner,
                        current_owner: owner,
                        requester_chain: current_chain,
                    };
                    self.runtime.send_message(registry_chain_id, message);
                }
            }
        }
    }

    async fn execute_message(&mut self, message: Self::Message) {
        let current_chain = self.runtime.chain_id();
        let registry_chain_id = self.state.registry_chain_id.get()
            .expect("Registry chain ID not set");

        match message {
            Message::RequestRegister { name, owner, requester_chain } => {
                // Only the registry chain should process registration requests
                assert_eq!(current_chain, registry_chain_id, "Only registry chain can process registrations");
                
                let existing = self.state.domains.get(&name).await.expect("Failed to read state");
                if existing.is_some() {
                    // Domain already taken - send failure response
                    let response = Message::RegistrationFailed {
                        name,
                        reason: "Domain already registered".to_string(),
                    };
                    self.runtime.send_message(requester_chain, response);
                } else {
                    // Register the domain
                    self.state.domains.insert(&name, owner).expect("Failed to register domain");
                    let response = Message::RegistrationSuccess { name };
                    self.runtime.send_message(requester_chain, response);
                }
            }
            Message::RequestTransfer { name, new_owner, current_owner, requester_chain } => {
                // Only the registry chain should process transfer requests
                assert_eq!(current_chain, registry_chain_id, "Only registry chain can process transfers");
                
                let stored_owner = self.state.domains.get(&name).await.expect("Failed to read state");
                match stored_owner {
                    None => {
                        let response = Message::TransferFailed {
                            name,
                            reason: "Domain not registered".to_string(),
                        };
                        self.runtime.send_message(requester_chain, response);
                    }
                    Some(owner) if owner != current_owner => {
                        let response = Message::TransferFailed {
                            name,
                            reason: "Not the domain owner".to_string(),
                        };
                        self.runtime.send_message(requester_chain, response);
                    }
                    Some(_) => {
                        // Transfer ownership
                        self.state.domains.insert(&name, new_owner.clone()).expect("Failed to transfer domain");
                        let response = Message::TransferSuccess { name, new_owner };
                        self.runtime.send_message(requester_chain, response);
                    }
                }
            }
            Message::RegistrationSuccess { name } => {
                // Received confirmation that registration succeeded
                // Could emit an event or update local cache here
                log::info!("Domain {} registered successfully", name);
            }
            Message::RegistrationFailed { name, reason } => {
                // Registration failed
                log::warn!("Domain {} registration failed: {}", name, reason);
            }
            Message::TransferSuccess { name, new_owner } => {
                // Transfer succeeded
                log::info!("Domain {} transferred to {}", name, new_owner);
            }
            Message::TransferFailed { name, reason } => {
                // Transfer failed
                log::warn!("Domain {} transfer failed: {}", name, reason);
            }
        }
    }

    async fn store(mut self) {
        self.state.save().await.expect("Failed to save state");
    }
}
```


**Tool Call: contracts/linera_name_system/src/service.rs**
Status: Completed



Diff: [PROJECT_ROOT]/linera-name-system/contracts/linera_name_system/src/service.rs
```
#![cfg_attr(target_arch = "wasm32", no_main)]

mod state;

use async_graphql::{EmptySubscription, Object, Request, Response, Schema};
use linera_sdk::{
    abi::WithServiceAbi,
    views::View,
    Service, ServiceRuntime,
};
use std::sync::Arc;

use linera_name_system::Operation;
use self::state::LineraNameSystemState;

pub struct LineraNameSystemService {
    state: Arc<LineraNameSystemState>,
    runtime: Arc<ServiceRuntime<Self>>,
}

linera_sdk::service!(LineraNameSystemService);

impl WithServiceAbi for LineraNameSystemService {
    type Abi = linera_name_system::LineraNameSystemAbi;
}

impl Service for LineraNameSystemService {
    type Parameters = ();

    async fn new(runtime: ServiceRuntime<Self>) -> Self {
        let state = LineraNameSystemState::load(runtime.root_view_storage_context())
            .await
            .expect("Failed to load state");
        LineraNameSystemService { 
            state: Arc::new(state),
            runtime: Arc::new(runtime),
        }
    }

    async fn handle_query(&self, request: Request) -> Response {
        let schema = Schema::build(QueryRoot, MutationRoot, EmptySubscription)
            .data(self.state.clone())
            .data(self.runtime.clone())
            .finish();
        schema.execute(request).await
    }
}

struct QueryRoot;

#[Object]
impl QueryRoot {
    /// Look up the owner of a domain
    async fn owner(&self, ctx: &async_graphql::Context<'_>, name: String) -> Option<String> {
        let state = ctx.data_unchecked::<Arc<LineraNameSystemState>>();
        state.domains.get(&name).await.ok().flatten()
    }

    /// Check if a domain is available
    async fn is_available(&self, ctx: &async_graphql::Context<'_>, name: String) -> bool {
        let state = ctx.data_unchecked::<Arc<LineraNameSystemState>>();
        state.domains.get(&name).await.ok().flatten().is_none()
    }

    /// Get the registry chain ID (the source of truth for all domains)
    async fn registry_chain_id(&self, ctx: &async_graphql::Context<'_>) -> Option<String> {
        let state = ctx.data_unchecked::<Arc<LineraNameSystemState>>();
        state.registry_chain_id.get().map(|id| id.to_string())
    }

    /// List all registered domains (only accurate on registry chain)
    async fn all_domains(&self, ctx: &async_graphql::Context<'_>) -> Vec<DomainInfo> {
        let state = ctx.data_unchecked::<Arc<LineraNameSystemState>>();
        let mut domains = Vec::new();
        let _ = state.domains.for_each_index_value(|name, owner| {
            domains.push(DomainInfo {
                name: name.clone(),
                owner: owner.clone(),
            });
            Ok(())
        }).await;
        domains
    }
}

#[derive(async_graphql::SimpleObject)]
struct DomainInfo {
    name: String,
    owner: String,
}

struct MutationRoot;

#[Object]
impl MutationRoot {
    /// Register a new .linera domain
    async fn register(&self, ctx: &async_graphql::Context<'_>, name: String) -> bool {
        let runtime = ctx.data_unchecked::<Arc<ServiceRuntime<LineraNameSystemService>>>();
        let operation = Operation::Register { name };
        runtime.schedule_operation(&operation);
        true
    }

    /// Transfer domain ownership
    async fn transfer(&self, ctx: &async_graphql::Context<'_>, name: String, new_owner: String) -> bool {
        let runtime = ctx.data_unchecked::<Arc<ServiceRuntime<LineraNameSystemService>>>();
        let operation = Operation::Transfer { name, new_owner };
        runtime.schedule_operation(&operation);
        true
    }
}
```

00001| "use client";
00002| 
00003| import { useCallback, useEffect, useRef, useState } from "react";
00004| import { useDynamicContext, useIsLoggedIn } from "@dynamic-labs/sdk-react-core";
00005| import { DynamicWidget } from "@dynamic-labs/sdk-react-core";
00006| import { lineraAdapter, type LineraProvider } from "@/lib/linera-adapter";
00007| 
00008| interface BlockLog {
00009|     height: number;
00010|     hash: string;
00011| }
00012| 
00013| interface DomainQueryResult {
00014|     Owner?: string | null;
00015|     IsAvailable?: boolean;
00016| }
00017| 
00018| export default function CounterApp() {
00019|     const { primaryWallet } = useDynamicContext();
00020|     const isLoggedIn = useIsLoggedIn();
00021|     const [mounted, setMounted] = useState(false);
00022|     const [chainId, setChainId] = useState<string | null>(null);
00023|     const [logs, setLogs] = useState<BlockLog[]>([]);
00024|     const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
00025| 
00026|     const providerRef = useRef<LineraProvider | null>(null);
00027|     const [chainConnected, setChainConnected] = useState(false);
00028|     const [appConnected, setAppConnected] = useState(false);
00029|     const [isAutoConnecting, setIsAutoConnecting] = useState(false);
00030| 
00031|     // Domain registration state
00032|     const [domainName, setDomainName] = useState("");
00033|     const [searchResult, setSearchResult] = useState<DomainQueryResult | null>(null);
00034|     const [isSearching, setIsSearching] = useState(false);
00035|     const [isRegistering, setIsRegistering] = useState(false);
00036| 
00037|     const applicationId = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_LINERA_APPLICATION_ID || "";
00038| 
00039|     useEffect(() => {
00040|         setMounted(true);
00041|         setChainConnected(lineraAdapter.isChainConnected());
00042|         setAppConnected(lineraAdapter.isApplicationSet());
00043|     }, []);
00044| 
00045|     // Auto-connect to Linera when wallet is connected
00046|     const autoConnect = useCallback(async () => {
00047|         if (!primaryWallet || !applicationId || isAutoConnecting) return;
00048|         if (chainConnected && appConnected) return;
00049| 
00050|         setIsAutoConnecting(true);
00051|         setError(null);
00052| 
00053|         try {
00054|             // Connect to Linera chain
00055|             if (!chainConnected) {
00056|                 const provider = await lineraAdapter.connect(primaryWallet);
00057|                 providerRef.current = provider;
00058|                 setChainConnected(true);
00059|                 setChainId(provider.chainId);
00060|             }
00061| 
00062|             // Connect to application
00063|             if (!appConnected && applicationId) {
00064|                 await lineraAdapter.setApplication(applicationId);
00065|                 setAppConnected(true);
00066|             }
00067|         } catch (err) {
00068|             console.error("Auto-connect failed:", err);
00069|             setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Failed to auto-connect to Linera");
00070|         } finally {
00071|             setIsAutoConnecting(false);
00072|         }
00073|     }, [primaryWallet, applicationId, chainConnected, appConnected, isAutoConnecting]);
00074| 
00075|     useEffect(() => {
00076|         if (mounted && isLoggedIn && primaryWallet && !chainConnected) {
00077|             autoConnect();
00078|         }
00079|     }, [mounted, isLoggedIn, primaryWallet, chainConnected, autoConnect]);
00080| 
00081|     // Reset Linera adapter when Dynamic wallet disconnects
00082|     useEffect(() => {
00083|         if (!isLoggedIn || !primaryWallet) {
00084|             lineraAdapter.reset();
00085|             providerRef.current = null;
00086|             setChainConnected(false);
00087|             setAppConnected(false);
00088|             setChainId(null);
00089|             setLogs([]);
00090|             setError(null);
00091|             setSearchResult(null);
00092|         }
00093|     }, [isLoggedIn, primaryWallet]);
00094| 
00095|     useEffect(() => {
00096|         if (!chainConnected || !providerRef.current) return;
00097|         const client = providerRef.current.client;
00098|         if (!client || typeof client.onNotification !== 'function') return;
00099| 
00100|         const handler = (notification: unknown) => {
00101|             const newBlock: BlockLog | undefined = (
00102|                 notification as { reason: { NewBlock: BlockLog } }
00103|             )?.reason?.NewBlock;
00104|             if (!newBlock) return;
00105|             setLogs((prev) => [newBlock, ...prev]);
00106|         };
00107| 
00108|         try {
00109|             client.onNotification(handler);
00110|         } catch (err) {
00111|             console.error('Failed to set notification handler:', err);
00112|         }
00113|         return () => { };
00114|     }, [chainConnected]);
00115| 
00116|     async function handleCheckDomain() {
00117|         if (!domainName.trim()) {
00118|             setError("Please enter a domain name");
00119|             return;
00120|         }
00121|         setIsSearching(true);
00122|         setError(null);
00123|         setSearchResult(null);
00124| 
00125|         try {
00126|             // GraphQL query for availability
00127|             const result = await lineraAdapter.queryApplication<{
00128|                 data?: { isAvailable: boolean };
00129|                 errors?: Array<{ message: string }>;
00130|             }>({
00131|                 query: `query { isAvailable(name: "${domainName.trim()}") }`
00132|             });
00133|             if (result.errors?.length) {
00134|                 throw new Error(result.errors[0].message);
00135|             }
00136|             setSearchResult({ IsAvailable: result.data?.isAvailable });
00137|         } catch (err) {
00138|             console.error("Failed to check domain:", err);
00139|             setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Failed to check domain availability");
00140|         } finally {
00141|             setIsSearching(false);
00142|         }
00143|     }
00144| 
00145|     async function handleRegisterDomain() {
00146|         if (!domainName.trim()) {
00147|             setError("Please enter a domain name");
00148|             return;
00149|         }
00150|         setIsRegistering(true);
00151|         setError(null);
00152| 
00153|         try {
00154|             // Call the register mutation - the service will schedule the operation
00155|             const result = await lineraAdapter.queryApplication<{
00156|                 data?: { register: boolean };
00157|                 errors?: Array<{ message: string }>;
00158|             }>({
00159|                 query: `mutation { register(name: "${domainName.trim()}") }`
00160|             });
00161| 
00162|             if (result.errors?.length) {
00163|                 throw new Error(result.errors[0].message);
00164|             }
00165| 
00166|             if (result.data?.register) {
00167|                 // Registration operation scheduled successfully
00168|                 setSearchResult({ IsAvailable: false });
00169|                 setError(null);
00170|                 // Show success message
00171|                 alert(`Domain ${domainName.trim()}.linera registration submitted! It may take a moment to be confirmed.`);
00172|             }
00173|         } catch (err) {
00174|             console.error("Failed to register domain:", err);
00175|             setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Failed to register domain");
00176|         } finally {
00177|             setIsRegistering(false);
00178|         }
00179|     }
00180| 
00181|     async function handleLookupOwner() {
00182|         if (!domainName.trim()) {
00183|             setError("Please enter a domain name");
00184|             return;
00185|         }
00186|         setIsSearching(true);
00187|         setError(null);
00188|         setSearchResult(null);
00189| 
00190|         try {
00191|             // GraphQL query for owner
00192|             const result = await lineraAdapter.queryApplication<{
00193|                 data?: { owner: string | null };
00194|                 errors?: Array<{ message: string }>;
00195|             }>({
00196|                 query: `query { owner(name: "${domainName.trim()}") }`
00197|             });
00198|             if (result.errors?.length) {
00199|                 throw new Error(result.errors[0].message);
00200|             }
00201|             setSearchResult({ Owner: result.data?.owner });
00202|         } catch (err) {
00203|             console.error("Failed to lookup owner:", err);
00204|             setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Failed to lookup domain owner");
00205|         } finally {
00206|             setIsSearching(false);
00207|         }
00208|     }
00209| 
00210|     return (
00211|         <div className="flex min-h-screen items-center justify-center bg-zinc-50 font-sans dark:bg-black">
00212|             <div className="w-full max-w-3xl px-6 py-12">

00216|                         <DynamicWidget />
00217|                     </div>
00218| 
00219|                     <div className="mb-8">
00220|                         <p className="mb-2 text-zinc-600 dark:text-zinc-400">
00221|                             Register your unique .linera domain on the Linera blockchain.
00222|                         </p>
00223|                         <p className="text-zinc-600 dark:text-zinc-400">
00224|                             Connect your wallet to get started. Your chain will be automatically claimed from the testnet faucet.
00225|                         </p>
00226|                     </div>
00227| 
00228|                     {error && (
00229|                         <div className="mb-6 rounded-lg bg-red-50 p-4 dark:bg-red-900/20">
00230|                             <p className="text-red-500 dark:text-red-300">{error}</p>
00231|                         </div>
00232|                     )}
00233| 
00234|                     {/* Connection Status */}

00236|                         <div className="mb-6 flex items-center justify-center gap-2 rounded-lg bg-sky-50 p-4 dark:bg-sky-900/20">
00237|                             <div className="h-4 w-4 animate-spin rounded-full border-2 border-sky-600 border-t-transparent" />
00238|                             <p className="text-sky-600 dark:text-sky-400">Connecting to Linera testnet...</p>
00239|                         </div>

```
"use client";

import { useCallback, useEffect, useRef, useState } from "react";
import { useDynamicContext, useIsLoggedIn } from "@dynamic-labs/sdk-react-core";
import { DynamicWidget } from "@dynamic-labs/sdk-react-core";
import { lineraAdapter, type LineraProvider } from "@/lib/linera-adapter";

interface BlockLog {
    height: number;
    hash: string;
}

interface DomainQueryResult {
    Owner?: string | null;
    IsAvailable?: boolean;
}

interface DomainInfo {
    name: string;
    owner: string;
}

export default function CounterApp() {
    const { primaryWallet } = useDynamicContext();
    const isLoggedIn = useIsLoggedIn();
    const [mounted, setMounted] = useState(false);
    const [chainId, setChainId] = useState<string | null>(null);
    const [registryChainId, setRegistryChainId] = useState<string | null>(null);
    const [logs, setLogs] = useState<BlockLog[]>([]);
    const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);

    const providerRef = useRef<LineraProvider | null>(null);
    const [chainConnected, setChainConnected] = useState(false);
    const [appConnected, setAppConnected] = useState(false);
    const [isAutoConnecting, setIsAutoConnecting] = useState(false);

    // Domain registration state
    const [domainName, setDomainName] = useState("");
    const [searchResult, setSearchResult] = useState<DomainQueryResult | null>(null);
    const [isSearching, setIsSearching] = useState(false);
    const [isRegistering, setIsRegistering] = useState(false);
    const [allDomains, setAllDomains] = useState<DomainInfo[]>([]);
    const [isLoadingDomains, setIsLoadingDomains] = useState(false);

    const applicationId = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_LINERA_APPLICATION_ID || "";
```

```
    // Reset Linera adapter when Dynamic wallet disconnects
    useEffect(() => {
        if (!isLoggedIn || !primaryWallet) {
            lineraAdapter.reset();
            providerRef.current = null;
            setChainConnected(false);
            setAppConnected(false);
            setChainId(null);
            setRegistryChainId(null);
            setLogs([]);
            setError(null);
            setSearchResult(null);
            setAllDomains([]);
        }
    }, [isLoggedIn, primaryWallet]);

Diff: [PROJECT_ROOT]/linera-name-system/src/components/counter-app.tsx
```
    async function handleLookupOwner() {
        if (!domainName.trim()) {
            setError("Please enter a domain name");
            return;
        }
        setIsSearching(true);
        setError(null);
        setSearchResult(null);

        try {
            // GraphQL query for owner
            const result = await lineraAdapter.queryApplication<{
                data?: { owner: string | null };
                errors?: Array<{ message: string }>;
            }>({
                query: `query { owner(name: "${domainName.trim()}") }`
            });
            if (result.errors?.length) {
                throw new Error(result.errors[0].message);
            }
            setSearchResult({ Owner: result.data?.owner });
        } catch (err) {
            console.error("Failed to lookup owner:", err);
            setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Failed to lookup domain owner");
        } finally {
            setIsSearching(false);
        }
    }

    // Fetch registry chain ID and all domains
    async function fetchRegistryInfo() {
        if (!appConnected) return;
        
        try {
            // Get registry chain ID
            const registryResult = await lineraAdapter.queryApplication<{
                data?: { registryChainId: string | null };
                errors?: Array<{ message: string }>;
            }>({
                query: `query { registryChainId }`
            });
            if (registryResult.data?.registryChainId) {
                setRegistryChainId(registryResult.data.registryChainId);
            }
        } catch (err) {
            console.error("Failed to fetch registry chain ID:", err);
        }
    }

    // Fetch all registered domains
    async function fetchAllDomains() {
        if (!appConnected) return;
        setIsLoadingDomains(true);
        
        try {
            const result = await lineraAdapter.queryApplication<{
                data?: { allDomains: DomainInfo[] };
                errors?: Array<{ message: string }>;
            }>({
                query: `query { allDomains { name owner } }`
            });
            if (result.errors?.length) {
                throw new Error(result.errors[0].message);
            }
            setAllDomains(result.data?.allDomains || []);
        } catch (err) {
            console.error("Failed to fetch all domains:", err);
        } finally {
            setIsLoadingDomains(false);
        }
    }

    // Fetch registry info when app is connected
    useEffect(() => {
        if (appConnected) {
            fetchRegistryInfo();
            fetchAllDomains();
        }
    }, [appConnected]);
```

00156|       setSearchResult({ IsAvailable: result.data?.isAvailable });
00157|     } catch (err) {
00158|       console.error("Failed to check domain:", err);
00159|       setError(
00160|         err instanceof Error
00161|           ? err.message
00162|           : "Failed to check domain availability",
00163|       );
00164|     } finally {
00165|       setIsSearching(false);
00166|     }
00167|   }
00168| 
00169|   async function handleRegisterDomain() {
00170|     if (!domainName.trim()) {
00171|       setError("Please enter a domain name");
00172|       return;
00173|     }
00174|     setIsRegistering(true);
00175|     setError(null);
00176| 
00177|     try {
00178|       // Call the register mutation - the service will schedule the operation
00179|       const result = await lineraAdapter.queryApplication<{
00180|         data?: { register: boolean };
00181|         errors?: Array<{ message: string }>;
00182|       }>({
00183|         query: `mutation { register(name: "${domainName.trim()}") }`,
00184|       });
00185| 
00186|       if (result.errors?.length) {
00187|         throw new Error(result.errors[0].message);
00188|       }
00189| 
00190|       if (result.data?.register) {
00191|         // Registration operation scheduled successfully
00192|         setSearchResult({ IsAvailable: false });
00193|         setError(null);
00194|         // Show success message
00195|         alert(
00196|           `Domain ${domainName.trim()}.linera registration submitted! It may take a moment to be confirmed.`,
00197|         );
00198|       }
00199|     } catch (err) {
00200|       console.error("Failed to register domain:", err);
00201|       setError(
00202|         err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Failed to register domain",
00203|       );

Diff: [PROJECT_ROOT]/linera-name-system/src/components/counter-app.tsx
```
"use client";

import { useCallback, useEffect, useRef, useState } from "react";
import { useDynamicContext, useIsLoggedIn } from "@dynamic-labs/sdk-react-core";
import { DynamicWidget } from "@dynamic-labs/sdk-react-core";
import { lineraAdapter, type LineraProvider } from "@/lib/linera-adapter";

interface BlockLog {
  height: number;
  hash: string;
}

interface DomainQueryResult {
  Owner?: string | null;
  IsAvailable?: boolean;
}

interface DomainInfo {
  name: string;
  owner: string;
}

export default function CounterApp() {
  const { primaryWallet } = useDynamicContext();
  const isLoggedIn = useIsLoggedIn();
  const [mounted, setMounted] = useState(false);
  const [chainId, setChainId] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [registryChainId, setRegistryChainId] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [logs, setLogs] = useState<BlockLog[]>([]);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);

  const providerRef = useRef<LineraProvider | null>(null);
  const [chainConnected, setChainConnected] = useState(false);
  const [appConnected, setAppConnected] = useState(false);
  const [isAutoConnecting, setIsAutoConnecting] = useState(false);

  // Domain registration state
  const [domainName, setDomainName] = useState("");
  const [searchResult, setSearchResult] = useState<DomainQueryResult | null>(null);
  const [isSearching, setIsSearching] = useState(false);
  const [isRegistering, setIsRegistering] = useState(false);
  const [allDomains, setAllDomains] = useState<DomainInfo[]>([]);
  const [isLoadingDomains, setIsLoadingDomains] = useState(false);

  const applicationId = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_LINERA_APPLICATION_ID || "";

  useEffect(() => {
    setMounted(true);
    setChainConnected(lineraAdapter.isChainConnected());
    setAppConnected(lineraAdapter.isApplicationSet());
  }, []);

  // Auto-connect to Linera when wallet is connected
  const autoConnect = useCallback(async () => {
    if (!primaryWallet || !applicationId || isAutoConnecting) return;
    if (chainConnected && appConnected) return;

    setIsAutoConnecting(true);
    setError(null);

    try {
      // Connect to Linera chain
      if (!chainConnected) {
        const provider = await lineraAdapter.connect(primaryWallet);
        providerRef.current = provider;
        setChainConnected(true);
        setChainId(provider.chainId);
      }

      // Connect to application
      if (!appConnected && applicationId) {
        await lineraAdapter.setApplication(applicationId);
        setAppConnected(true);
      }
    } catch (err) {
      console.error("Auto-connect failed:", err);
      setError(
        err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Failed to auto-connect to Linera"
      );
    } finally {
      setIsAutoConnecting(false);
    }
  }, [primaryWallet, applicationId, chainConnected, appConnected, isAutoConnecting]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (mounted && isLoggedIn && primaryWallet && !chainConnected) {
      autoConnect();
    }
  }, [mounted, isLoggedIn, primaryWallet, chainConnected, autoConnect]);

  // Reset Linera adapter when Dynamic wallet disconnects
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!isLoggedIn || !primaryWallet) {
      lineraAdapter.reset();
      providerRef.current = null;
      setChainConnected(false);
      setAppConnected(false);
      setChainId(null);
      setRegistryChainId(null);
      setLogs([]);
      setError(null);
      setSearchResult(null);
      setAllDomains([]);
    }
  }, [isLoggedIn, primaryWallet]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!chainConnected || !providerRef.current) return;
    const client = providerRef.current.client;
    if (!client || typeof client.onNotification !== "function") return;

    const handler = (notification: unknown) => {
      const newBlock: BlockLog | undefined = (
        notification as { reason: { NewBlock: BlockLog } }
      )?.reason?.NewBlock;
      if (!newBlock) return;
      setLogs((prev) => [newBlock, ...prev]);
    };

    try {
      client.onNotification(handler);
    } catch (err) {
      console.error("Failed to set notification handler:", err);
    }
    return () => {};
  }, [chainConnected]);

  // Fetch registry chain ID
  const fetchRegistryInfo = useCallback(async () => {
    if (!appConnected) return;

    try {
      const registryResult = await lineraAdapter.queryApplication<{
        data?: { registryChainId: string | null };
        errors?: Array<{ message: string }>;
      }>({
        query: `query { registryChainId }`,
      });
      if (registryResult.data?.registryChainId) {
        setRegistryChainId(registryResult.data.registryChainId);
      }
    } catch (err) {
      console.error("Failed to fetch registry chain ID:", err);
    }
  }, [appConnected]);

  // Fetch all registered domains
  const fetchAllDomains = useCallback(async () => {
    if (!appConnected) return;
    setIsLoadingDomains(true);

    try {
      const result = await lineraAdapter.queryApplication<{
        data?: { allDomains: DomainInfo[] };
        errors?: Array<{ message: string }>;
      }>({
        query: `query { allDomains { name owner } }`,
      });
      if (result.errors?.length) {
        throw new Error(result.errors[0].message);
      }
      setAllDomains(result.data?.allDomains || []);
    } catch (err) {
      console.error("Failed to fetch all domains:", err);
    } finally {
      setIsLoadingDomains(false);
    }
  }, [appConnected]);

  // Fetch registry info when app is connected
  useEffect(() => {
    if (appConnected) {
      fetchRegistryInfo();
      fetchAllDomains();
    }
  }, [appConnected, fetchRegistryInfo, fetchAllDomains]);

  async function handleCheckDomain() {
    if (!domainName.trim()) {
      setError("Please enter a domain name");
      return;
    }
    setIsSearching(true);
    setError(null);
    setSearchResult(null);

    try {
      const result = await lineraAdapter.queryApplication<{
        data?: { isAvailable: boolean };
        errors?: Array<{ message: string }>;
      }>({
        query: `query { isAvailable(name: "${domainName.trim()}") }`,
      });
      if (result.errors?.length) {
        throw new Error(result.errors[0].message);
      }
      setSearchResult({ IsAvailable: result.data?.isAvailable });
    } catch (err) {
      console.error("Failed to check domain:", err);
      setError(
        err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Failed to check domain availability"
      );
    } finally {
      setIsSearching(false);
    }
  }

  async function handleRegisterDomain() {
    if (!domainName.trim()) {
      setError("Please enter a domain name");
      return;
    }
    setIsRegistering(true);
    setError(null);

    try {
      const result = await lineraAdapter.queryApplication<{
        data?: { register: boolean };
        errors?: Array<{ message: string }>;
      }>({
        query: `mutation { register(name: "${domainName.trim()}") }`,
      });

      if (result.errors?.length) {
        throw new Error(result.errors[0].message);
      }

      if (result.data?.register) {
        setSearchResult({ IsAvailable: false });
        setError(null);
        alert(
          `Domain ${domainName.trim()}.linera registration submitted! It may take a moment to be confirmed.`
        );
        // Refresh domains list after registration
        setTimeout(() => fetchAllDomains(), 2000);
      }
    } catch (err) {
      console.error("Failed to register domain:", err);
      setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Failed to register domain");
    } finally {
      setIsRegistering(false);
    }
  }

  async function handleLookupOwner() {
    if (!domainName.trim()) {
      setError("Please enter a domain name");
      return;
    }
    setIsSearching(true);
    setError(null);
    setSearchResult(null);

    try {
      const result = await lineraAdapter.queryApplication<{
        data?: { owner: string | null };
        errors?: Array<{ message: string }>;
      }>({
        query: `query { owner(name: "${domainName.trim()}") }`,
      });
      if (result.errors?.length) {
        throw new Error(result.errors[0].message);
      }
      setSearchResult({ Owner: result.data?.owner });
    } catch (err) {
      console.error("Failed to lookup owner:", err);
      setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Failed to lookup domain owner");
    } finally {
      setIsSearching(false);
    }
  }

  return (
    <div className="flex min-h-screen items-center justify-center bg-zinc-50 font-sans dark:bg-black">
      <div className="w-full max-w-3xl px-6 py-12">
        <div className="rounded-xl bg-white p-8 shadow-lg dark:bg-zinc-900">
          <div className="mb-8 flex items-center justify-between">
            <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold text-zinc-900 dark:text-white">
              Linera Name System
            </h1>
            <DynamicWidget />
          </div>

          <div className="mb-8">
            <p className="mb-2 text-zinc-600 dark:text-zinc-400">
              Register your unique .linera domain on the Linera blockchain.
            </p>
            <p className="text-zinc-600 dark:text-zinc-400">
              Connect your wallet to get started. Your chain will be
              automatically claimed from the testnet faucet.
            </p>
          </div>

          {error && (
            <div className="mb-6 rounded-lg bg-red-50 p-4 dark:bg-red-900/20">
              <p className="text-red-500 dark:text-red-300">{error}</p>
            </div>
          )}

          {/* Connection Status */}
          {mounted && isAutoConnecting && (
            <div className="mb-6 flex items-center justify-center gap-2 rounded-lg bg-sky-50 p-4 dark:bg-sky-900/20">
              <div className="h-4 w-4 animate-spin rounded-full border-2 border-sky-600 border-t-transparent" />
              <p className="text-sky-600 dark:text-sky-400">
                Connecting to Linera testnet...
              </p>
            </div>
          )}

          {mounted && !isLoggedIn && (
            <div className="mb-6 rounded-lg bg-zinc-100 p-6 text-center dark:bg-zinc-800">
              <p className="text-zinc-500 dark:text-zinc-400">
                Please connect your wallet using the button above to get started.
              </p>
            </div>
          )}

          {/* Domain Registration UI */}
          {chainConnected && appConnected && (
            <div className="space-y-6">
              <div className="rounded-lg bg-zinc-100 p-6 dark:bg-zinc-800">
                <h2 className="mb-4 text-lg font-semibold text-zinc-900 dark:text-white">
                  Search & Register Domain
                </h2>
                <div className="flex gap-2">
                  <div className="relative flex-1">
                    <input
                      type="text"
                      value={domainName}
                      onChange={(e) =>
                        setDomainName(
                          e.target.value.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9-]/g, "")
                        )
                      }
                      placeholder="Enter domain name"
                      className="w-full rounded-lg border border-zinc-300 bg-white px-4 py-3 pr-20 text-zinc-900 placeholder-zinc-400 focus:border-sky-500 focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-sky-500 dark:border-zinc-600 dark:bg-zinc-900 dark:text-white dark:placeholder-zinc-500"
                    />
                    <span className="absolute right-4 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-zinc-400 dark:text-zinc-500">
                      .linera
                    </span>
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div className="mt-4 flex gap-2">
                  <button
                    type="button"
                    onClick={handleCheckDomain}
                    disabled={isSearching || !domainName.trim()}
                    className="flex-1 rounded-lg bg-zinc-200 px-4 py-2 font-medium text-zinc-800 transition-colors hover:bg-zinc-300 disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:opacity-50 dark:bg-zinc-700 dark:text-zinc-200 dark:hover:bg-zinc-600"
                  >
                    {isSearching ? "Checking..." : "Check Availability"}
                  </button>
                  <button
                    type="button"
                    onClick={handleLookupOwner}
                    disabled={isSearching || !domainName.trim()}
                    className="flex-1 rounded-lg bg-zinc-200 px-4 py-2 font-medium text-zinc-800 transition-colors hover:bg-zinc-300 disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:opacity-50 dark:bg-zinc-700 dark:text-zinc-200 dark:hover:bg-zinc-600"
                  >
                    Lookup Owner
                  </button>
                </div>

                {searchResult && (
                  <div className="mt-4 rounded-lg bg-white p-4 dark:bg-zinc-900">
                    {searchResult.IsAvailable !== undefined && (
                      <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
                        <div>
                          <p className="font-medium text-zinc-900 dark:text-white">
                            {domainName}.linera
                          </p>
                          <p
                            className={
                              searchResult.IsAvailable
                                ? "text-green-600 dark:text-green-400"
                                : "text-red-600 dark:text-red-400"
                            }
                          >
                            {searchResult.IsAvailable
                              ? "Available!"
                              : "Already registered"}
                          </p>
                        </div>
                        {searchResult.IsAvailable && (
                          <button
                            type="button"
                            onClick={handleRegisterDomain}
                            disabled={isRegistering}
                            className="rounded-lg bg-sky-600 px-6 py-2 font-medium text-white transition-colors hover:bg-sky-700 disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:opacity-50"
                          >
                            {isRegistering ? "Registering..." : "Register"}
                          </button>
                        )}
                      </div>
                    )}
                    {searchResult.Owner !== undefined && (
                      <div>
                        <p className="font-medium text-zinc-900 dark:text-white">
                          {domainName}.linera
                        </p>
                        <p className="text-sm text-zinc-500 dark:text-zinc-400">
                          Owner:
                        </p>
                        <p className="break-all font-mono text-sm text-zinc-700 dark:text-zinc-300">
                          {searchResult.Owner || "Not registered"}
                        </p>
                      </div>
                    )}
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>

              {/* All Registered Domains */}
              <div className="rounded-lg bg-zinc-100 p-6 dark:bg-zinc-800">
                <div className="mb-4 flex items-center justify-between">
                  <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold text-zinc-900 dark:text-white">
                    Registered Domains
                  </h2>
                  <button
                    type="button"
                    onClick={fetchAllDomains}
                    disabled={isLoadingDomains}
                    className="rounded-lg bg-zinc-200 px-3 py-1 text-sm font-medium text-zinc-700 transition-colors hover:bg-zinc-300 disabled:opacity-50 dark:bg-zinc-700 dark:text-zinc-300 dark:hover:bg-zinc-600"
                  >
                    {isLoadingDomains ? "Loading..." : "Refresh"}
                  </button>
                </div>
                {allDomains.length === 0 ? (
                  <p className="text-zinc-500 dark:text-zinc-400">
                    {isLoadingDomains ? "Loading domains..." : "No domains registered yet."}
                  </p>
                ) : (
                  <ul className="max-h-48 space-y-2 overflow-y-auto">
                    {allDomains.map((domain) => (
                      <li
                        key={domain.name}
                        className="rounded-lg bg-white p-3 dark:bg-zinc-900"
                      >
                        <p className="font-medium text-zinc-900 dark:text-white">
                          {domain.name}.linera
                        </p>
                        <p className="truncate text-xs text-zinc-500 dark:text-zinc-400">
                          Owner: {domain.owner.slice(0, 16)}...{domain.owner.slice(-8)}
                        </p>
                      </li>
                    ))}
                  </ul>
                )}
              </div>
            </div>
          )}

          {/* Chain Info */}
          {chainConnected && (
            <div className="mt-8 space-y-4 border-t border-zinc-200 pt-6 dark:border-zinc-700">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                <div className="h-2 w-2 rounded-full bg-green-500" />
                <span className="text-sm text-zinc-600 dark:text-zinc-400">
                  Connected to Linera Testnet
                </span>
              </div>
              <div className="space-y-2 text-sm">
                <p className="text-zinc-700 dark:text-zinc-300">
                  <span className="font-medium">Your Chain ID:</span>{" "}
                  <code className="break-all rounded bg-zinc-100 px-2 py-1 font-mono text-xs text-zinc-600 dark:bg-zinc-800 dark:text-zinc-400">
                    {chainId ? `${chainId.slice(0, 16)}...${chainId.slice(-8)}` : "..."}
                  </code>
                </p>
                {registryChainId && (
                  <p className="text-zinc-700 dark:text-zinc-300">
                    <span className="font-medium">Registry Chain ID:</span>{" "}
                    <code className="break-all rounded bg-zinc-100 px-2 py-1 font-mono text-xs text-zinc-600 dark:bg-zinc-800 dark:text-zinc-400">
                      {registryChainId.slice(0, 16)}...{registryChainId.slice(-8)}
                    </code>
                  </p>
                )}
                <p className="text-zinc-500 dark:text-zinc-500">
                  Application ID:{" "}
                  <code className="break-all font-mono text-xs">
                    {applicationId.slice(0, 16)}...{applicationId.slice(-8)}
                  </code>
                </p>
              </div>

              {logs.length > 0 && (
                <>
                  <h3 className="text-sm font-semibold text-zinc-700 dark:text-zinc-300">
                    Recent Blocks
                  </h3>
                  <ul className="max-h-32 space-y-1 overflow-y-auto">
                    {logs.slice(0, 5).map((log, index) => (
                      <li
                        key={`${log.hash}-${index}`}
                        className="rounded bg-zinc-100 px-2 py-1 font-mono text-xs dark:bg-zinc-800"
                      >
                        <span className="font-semibold text-zinc-700 dark:text-zinc-300">
                          {log.height}
                        </span>
                        :{" "}
                        <span className="text-zinc-500 dark:text-zinc-500">
                          {log.hash.slice(0, 16)}...
                        </span>
                      </li>
                    ))}
                  </ul>
                </>
              )}
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

```

## Assistant

The implementation is complete. Here's a summary of what was done:

## Summary

### Smart Contract Changes (Cross-Chain Messaging)

1. **`lib.rs`** - Added `Message` enum for cross-chain communication:
   - `RequestRegister` - Sent from user chains to registry chain
   - `RequestTransfer` - Sent from user chains to registry chain
   - `RegistrationSuccess/Failed` - Response messages
   - `TransferSuccess/Failed` - Response messages

2. **`state.rs`** - Added `registry_chain_id` field to track the source of truth chain

3. **`contract.rs`** - Implemented the Hub-and-Spoke pattern:
   - On `instantiate()`: Sets the deploying chain as the registry chain
   - On `execute_operation()`: 
     - If on registry chain: Execute directly
     - If on user chain: Send cross-chain message to registry
   - On `execute_message()`: Process registration/transfer requests on registry chain

4. **`service.rs`** - Added new GraphQL queries:
   - `registryChainId` - Returns the registry chain ID
   - `allDomains` - Lists all registered domains (accurate on registry chain)

### Frontend Changes

- Added display of registry chain ID
- Added "Registered Domains" section showing all domains
- Added refresh button to reload domain list
- Auto-fetches registry info and domains on connection

### Deployment

- **New Application ID**: `2dd9a653d0418798995a043b511dc5853fb2dfef558bc1c12ded374b3b70a5c2`
- **Registry Chain ID**: `165f2f8a389e61d870d0afa52803643df413e4d085aef63666bd8fd9fce4ffcc` (the chain that deployed the contract)

### How It Works Now

1. **Reading**: All users query the registry chain to see the global list of domains
2. **Writing**: When a user registers a domain:
   - If they're on the registry chain: Direct registration
   - If they're on their own chain: A cross-chain message is sent to the registry chain, which processes it and sends back a confirmation

This ensures all domain registrations are synchronized through the single registry chain, preventing conflicts where two users could claim the same domain on different chains.

got this error on [@debug](file://[PROJECT_ROOT]/linera-name-system/src/app/debug) when trying to register a domain please fix

## Assistant

The error shows a panic in the contract, likely from the `assert!` on `registry_chain_id.get()`. The issue is that when a user connects from their own chain (not the registry chain), the `registry_chain_id` is `None` because the state was never initialized on their chain.

Let me fix this by making the contract handle the case where it's running on a non-registry chain that doesn't have the registry chain ID stored locally.

00041|         // This chain becomes the "source of truth" for all domain registrations

00043|         self.state.registry_chain_id.set(Some(registry_chain_id));
